Condition.</span></td></tr></table></div><div style="text-indent:24.75pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">On December&#160;5, 2024, lululemon athletica inc. (the "Company") issued a press release announcing its financial results for the third quarter ended October&#160;27, 2024 and certain other information. A copy of the Company's press release is attached hereto as Exhibit 99.1 and is incorporated herein by reference. As previously announced, the Company has scheduled a conference call for 4:30 p.m. Eastern time on December&#160;5, 2024 to discuss its financial results. </span></div><div style="margin-top:10pt"><table style="border-collapse:collapse;display:inline-table;margin-bottom:5pt;vertical-align:text-bottom;width:99.853%"><tr><td style="width:1.0%"/><td style="width:9.880%"/><td style="width:0.1%"/><td style="width:1.0%"/><td style="width:87.920%"/><td style="width:0.1%"/></tr><tr><td colspan="3" style="padding:2px 1pt;text-align:left;vertical-align:top"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:100%">Item&#160;8.01.</span></td><td colspan="3" style="padding:2px 1pt;text-align:left;vertical-align:top"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:100%">Other Events.</span></td></tr></table></div><div style="margin-top:5pt;text-indent:24.75pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">On December&#160;3, 2024, the board of directors approved a $1.0 billion increase to the Company's existing stock repurchase program. The repurchase authorization has no time limit and does not require the repurchase of a minimum number of shares. Common shares may be repurchased on the open market, in block trades, or in privately negotiated transactions, including under plans complying with the provisions of Rule 10b5-1 and Rule 10b-18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934. The timing and actual number of common shares to be repurchased will depend upon market conditions, eligibility to trade, and other factors.   </span></div><div style="margin-top:10pt"><table (NASDAQ&#58;LULU) today announced financial results for the third quarter of fiscal 2024, which ended on October&#160;27, 2024.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Calvin McDonald, Chief Executive Officer, stated&#58; &#34;Our performance in the third quarter shows the enduring strength of lululemon globally, as we saw continued momentum across our international markets and in Canada. Thank you to our dedicated teams for continuing to deliver for our guests and stakeholders.&#34;</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:9pt"><font recognized in relation to lululemon Studio during the third quarter of 2023, and the related income tax effects of these items.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:9pt"><font dollar basis.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:3pt;padding-left:40.5pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8211;</font><font basis.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:3pt;padding-left:22.5pt;text-indent:-22.5pt"><font basis.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;padding-left:22.5pt;text-indent:-22.5pt"><font Adjusted gross profit increased 9%.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;padding-left:22.5pt;text-indent:-22.5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:17.52pt">Gross margin increased 150 basis points to 58.5%. Adjusted gross margin increased 40 basis points.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;padding-left:22.5pt;text-indent:-22.5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:17.52pt">Income from operations increased 45% to $490.7 million. Adjusted income from operations increased 12%. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;padding-left:22.5pt;text-indent:-22.5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:17.52pt">Operating margin increased 520 basis points to 20.5%. Adjusted operating margin increased 70 basis points.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;padding-left:22.5pt;text-indent:-22.5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:17.52pt">The effective income tax rate for the third quarter of 2024 was 30.2% compared to 28.5% for the third quarter of 2023. The adjusted effective tax rate was 28.1% for the third quarter of 2023.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;padding-left:22.5pt;text-indent:-22.5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:17.52pt">Diluted earnings per share were $2.87 compared to $1.96 in the third quarter of 2023. Adjusted diluted earnings per share were $2.53 in the third quarter of 2023.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;padding-left:22.5pt;text-indent:-22.5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:17.52pt">The Company added 28 new company-operated stores during the third quarter, including 14 company-operated stores from the acquisition of the Mexico operations, ending with 749 stores.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Meghan Frank, Chief Financial Officer, stated&#58; &#34;Our third quarter results, which exceeded our expectations, demonstrate the ability of our teams to be agile in a dynamic operating environment. With the majority of the fourth quarter still in front of us, we are focused on deepening engagement with our guests and bringing new consumers into the brand. We are committed to delivering on our Power of Three &#215;2 revenue target of $12.5 billion in 2026 and look forward to all that lies ahead.&#34;</font></div><div style="margin-top:14pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Stock Repurchase Program</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">During the third quarter of 2024, the Company repurchased 1.6 million shares of its common stock for a cost of $408.5 million. </font></div><div style="height:63pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div style="margin-top:9pt;text-align:center"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">1</font></div></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:99pt;width:100%"><div style="text-align:center"><font><br></font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-top:5pt;text-align:center;text-indent:27pt"><img alt="lululemon_corexlockupxblacka.jpg" src="lululemon_corexlockupxblacka.jpg" style="height:36px;margin-bottom:5pt;vertical-align:text-bottom;width:258px"></div></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">On December&#160;3, 2024, the board of directors approved a $1.0 billion increase to the Company's stock repurchase program. Including this increase, as of December&#160;5, 2024, the Company had approximately $1.8 billion remaining authorized on its stock repurchase program.</font></div><div style="margin-top:14pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Balance Sheet Highlights</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">The Company ended the third quarter of 2024 with $1.2 billion in cash and cash equivalents and the capacity under its committed revolving credit facility was $393.5 million. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Inventories at the end of the third quarter of 2024 increased 8% to $1.8 billion compared to $1.7 billion at the end of the third quarter of 2023.</font></div><div id="i3ea0867bc93e4c0ea9cb9a26dec20182_7"></div><div style="margin-top:14pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">2024 Outlook</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">For the fourth quarter of 2024, the Company expects net revenue to be in the range of $3.475 billion to $3.510 billion, representing growth of 8% to 10%, or 3% to 4% excluding the 53rd week of 2024. Diluted earnings per share are expected to be in the range of $5.56 to $5.64 for the quarter. This assumes a tax rate of approximately 29.5%.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">For 2024, the Company now expects net revenue to be in the range of $10.452 billion to $10.487 billion, representing growth of 9%, or 7% excluding the 53rd week of 2024. Diluted earnings per share are now expected to be in the range of $14.08 to $14.16 for the year. This assumes a tax rate of approximately 30%.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">The guidance does not reflect potential future repurchases of the Company's shares.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">The guidance and outlook forward-looking statements made in this press release are based on management's expectations as of the date of this press release and do not incorporate future unknown impacts, including macroeconomic trends. The Company undertakes no duty to update or to continue to provide information with respect to any forward-looking statements or risk factors, whether as a result of new information or future events or circumstances or otherwise. Actual results and the timing of events could differ materially from those anticipated in these forward-looking statements as a result of risks and uncertainties, including those stated below.</font></div><div id="i3ea0867bc93e4c0ea9cb9a26dec20182_13"></div><div style="margin-top:14pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Power of Three &#215;2</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">The Company's Power of Three &#215;2 growth plan calls for a doubling of the business from 2021 net revenue of $6.25 billion to $12.5 billion by 2026. The key pillars of the plan are product innovation, guest experience, and market expansion.</font></div><div style="margin-top:14pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Conference Call Information</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">A conference call to discuss third quarter results is scheduled for today, December&#160;5, 2024, at 4&#58;30 p.m. Eastern time. Those interested in participating in the call are invited to dial 1-844-763-8274 or 1-647-484-8814, if calling internationally, approximately 10 minutes prior to the start of the call. A live webcast of the conference call will be available online at&#58; https&#58;&#47;&#47;corporate.lululemon.com&#47;investors&#47;news-and-events&#47;events-and-presentations. A replay will be made available online approximately two hours following the live call for a period of 30 days.</font></div><div style="margin-top:14pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">About lululemon athletica inc.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">lululemon athletica inc. (NASDAQ&#58;LULU) is a technical athletic apparel, footwear, and accessories company for yoga, running, training, and most other activities, creating transformational products and experiences that build meaningful connections, unlocking greater possibility and wellbeing for all.&#160;Setting the bar in innovation of fabrics and functional designs, lululemon works with yogis and athletes in local communities around the world for continuous research and product feedback.&#160;For more information, visit lululemon.com.</font></div><div style="height:63pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="height:36px;margin-bottom:5pt;vertical-align:text-bottom;width:258px"></div></div><div style="margin-top:14pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Non-GAAP Financial Measures</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Constant dollar changes and adjusted financial results are non-GAAP financial measures. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">A constant dollar basis assumes the average foreign currency exchange rates for the period remained constant with the average foreign currency exchange rates for the same period of the prior year. The Company provides constant dollar changes in its results to help investors understand the underlying growth rate of net revenue excluding the impact of changes in foreign currency exchange rates. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Adjusted gross profit, gross margin, income from operations, operating margin, income tax expense, effective tax rates, net income, and diluted earnings per share exclude certain inventory provisions, asset impairments, and restructuring costs recognized in relation to lululemon Studio, and the related income tax effects of these items. The Company believes these adjusted financial measures are useful to investors as they provide supplemental information that enable evaluation of the underlying trend in its operating performance, and enable a comparison to its historical financial information. Further, due to the finite and discrete nature of these items, it does not consider them to be normal operating expenses that are necessary to run the business, or impairments or disposal gains that are expected to arise in the normal course of its operations. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Management uses these adjusted financial measures and constant currency metrics internally when reviewing and assessing financial performance.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">The Company's fiscal year ends on the Sunday closest to January&#160;31st of the following year, typically resulting in a 52-week year, but occasionally giving rise to an additional week, resulting in a 53-week year. Fiscal 2023 was a 52-week year while 2024 will be a 53-week year. The expected net revenue increase excluding the 53rd week excludes the expected net revenue for the 53rd week of 2024. This enables an evaluation of the expected year-over-year increase in net revenue based on 52 weeks in each year.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">The presentation of this financial information is not intended to be considered in isolation or as a substitute for, or with greater prominence to, the financial information prepared and presented in accordance with GAAP. For more information on these non-GAAP financial measures, please see the section captioned &#34;Reconciliation of Non-GAAP Financial Measures&#34; included in the accompanying financial tables, which includes more detail on the GAAP financial measure that is most directly comparable to each non-GAAP financial measure, and the related reconciliations between these financial measures. The Company's non-GAAP financial measures may be calculated differently from, and therefore may not be directly comparable to, similarly titled measures reported by other companies.</font></div><div style="margin-top:14pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Forward-Looking Statements&#58; </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">This press release includes estimates, projections, statements relating to the Company's business plans, objectives, and expected operating results that are &#34;forward-looking statements&#34; within the meaning of the Private Securities Litigation Reform Act of 1995, Section 27A of the Securities Act of 1933 and Section 21E of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934.
